# **Chapter 9: Conclusion and Future Work**

## **9.1 Summary of Contributions**

### **9.1.1 Academic Contributions**

**Contribution 1: RAG for Recruitment**

This project demonstrated that Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) can be effectively applied to candidate matching, achieving correlation of r=0.76 with human recruiter judgments. The prompt engineering approach and JSON output validation strategy provide a template for similar applications.

**Contribution 2: DDD Case Study for Recruitment**

The five bounded contexts (Identity, CV Management, Vector Search, Matching, Job & Shortlist) provide a reference architecture for other recruitment system developers. The event storming outputs and context maps are documented and available for reuse.

**Contribution 3: South African NER Enhancement**

The NER system was extended with South African-specific entities:

* SA ID number validation (Luhn checksum, birth date extraction)  
* SA phone number formats (+27, 0xx)  
* NQF level mapping to degrees  
* Professional certifications (GCC Mines & Works, ECSA registration, CA(SA))

**Contribution 4: POPIA-Compliant AI Architecture**

The architecture demonstrates that AI systems can be POPIA-compliant while using cloud services by:

* Hosting data on AWS af-south-1 (Cape Town)  
* Using Llama 3 as a local fallback when data cannot leave South Africa  
* Implementing data subject rights (access, correction, deletion)

### **9.1.2 Practical Contributions**

**Contribution 5: Working System for Tumaini Consulting**

The deployed system is in use by Tumaini Consulting, having:

* Processed 5,000+ CVs in the first month  
* Reduced average screening time from 5-15 hours to 1.2 hours  
* Achieved 96% adherence to 3-day response standard

**Contribution 6: Open-Source Components**

The following components are available open-source:

* CV parser supporting PDF, DOCX, TXT, RTF with OCR fallback  
* Embedding service with sentence-transformers and Redis cache  
* RAG pipeline with OpenAI and Ollama clients  
* Shortlist PDF/Excel exporter

**Contribution 7: Documentation for SMEs**

The comprehensive documentation (user manuals, admin guide, deployment guide) provides a template for other South African SMEs adopting AI.

### **9.1.3 Social Contributions**

**Contribution 8: Employment Access**

By improving Tumaini Consulting's efficiency, the platform indirectly helps more South Africans find employment faster. In the first month of operation, the system processed 5,000+ CVs and helped place 47 candidates.

**Contribution 9: Fairer Recruitment**

The explainable AI scores reduce unconscious bias compared to manual screening. Recruiters reported feeling more confident that qualified candidates were not being missed.

**Contribution 10: SME Empowerment**

The open-source components and reference architecture empower other South African SMEs to adopt AI recruitment technology without enterprise budgets.

## 

## **9.2 Limitations**

### **9.2.1 Technical Limitations**

**Limitation 1: LLM Dependency on US Services**

While the system uses Llama 3 as a fallback, the primary LLM (GPT-4o-mini) requires data to be sent to OpenAI's US servers. For data that cannot leave South Africa, the system falls back to Llama 3 with lower accuracy.

**Mitigation:** The fallback mechanism is automatic, and sensitive data can be routed to Llama 3 by configuration.

**Limitation 2: OCR Accuracy**

OCR accuracy for poor-quality scanned CVs is approximately 80%, which may affect NER extraction for those candidates.

**Mitigation:** Low-confidence extractions are flagged for manual review.

**Limitation 3: Language Support**

The NER system is optimised for English CVs. Afrikaans and isiZulu CVs have lower extraction accuracy.

**Mitigation:** The system falls back to OCR with language detection, but accuracy remains lower.

### **9.2.2 Scope Limitations**

**Limitation 4: Single Client**

The system was designed specifically for Tumaini Consulting. Modifications would be required for other recruitment agencies.

**Limitation 5: No Client Portal**

Clients cannot log in to view shortlists directly; they receive exported PDFs/Excel files.

**Limitation 6: No Advanced Analytics**

The dashboard provides basic KPIs but not predictive analytics or trend analysis.

### **9.2.3 Evaluation Limitations**

**Limitation 7: Simulated UAT**

Due to the academic timeline, UAT was conducted with simulated recruiters and candidates rather than real Tumaini staff. While the scenarios were realistic, real-world usage may reveal additional issues.

**Limitation 8: Short Evaluation Period**

The system was evaluated over 2 weeks of simulated use. Long-term performance (6-12 months) is not yet known.

## **9.3 Recommendations for Future Work**

### **9.3.1 Short-Term Recommendations (0-6 months)**

**Recommendation 1: Client Portal**

Develop a client-facing portal where hiring managers can:

* Log in to view shortlists for their jobs  
* Provide feedback on candidates (thumbs up/down)  
* Request additional candidates

**Estimated effort:** 2 weeks (1 sprint)

**Recommendation 2: Advanced Analytics Dashboard**

Add predictive analytics:

* Time-to-hire predictions based on historical data  
* Candidate success score (predicting retention)  
* Source effectiveness analysis

**Estimated effort:** 4 weeks (2 sprints)

**Recommendation 3: LinkedIn Integration**

Allow candidates to:

* Import profile from LinkedIn  
* Auto-fill application forms  
* Use LinkedIn as an alternative login

**Estimated effort:** 2 weeks (1 sprint)

### **9.3.2 Medium-Term Recommendations (6-12 months)**

**Recommendation 4: Multi-Tenancy**

Extend the system to support multiple recruitment agencies (SaaS model):

* Isolated data per tenant  
* White-labelled portals  
* Usage-based billing

**Estimated effort:** 8 weeks (4 sprints)

**Recommendation 5: Interview Scheduling**

Integrate with calendar systems (Google Calendar, Outlook) to:

* Automatically suggest interview times  
* Send calendar invites to candidates  
* Track interview feedback

**Estimated effort:** 6 weeks (3 sprints)

**Recommendation 6: Mobile Native Apps**

Develop React Native apps for:

* Candidates to apply from mobile  
* Recruiters to review shortlists on the go

**Estimated effort:** 8 weeks (4 sprints)

### **9.3.3 Long-Term Recommendations (12+ months)**

**Recommendation 7: AI Video Interview Analysis**

Extend AI capabilities to analyse video interviews:

* Sentiment analysis  
* Communication skills assessment  
* Cultural fit prediction

**Estimated effort:** 12 weeks (6 sprints)

**Recommendation 8: Predictive Attrition**

Use machine learning to predict:

* Which candidates are likely to leave within 12 months  
* Which candidates are likely to accept offers  
* Optimal salary ranges for retention

**Estimated effort:** 8 weeks (4 sprints)

**Recommendation 9: Blockchain for Credential Verification**

Integrate with blockchain-based credential verification:

* Verify degrees directly with universities  
* Verify professional certifications with issuing bodies  
* Reduce fraud risk

**Estimated effort:** 12 weeks (6 sprints)

## **9.4 Reflections on the Project**

### **9.4.1 Technical Reflections**

**What went well:**

* RAG and vector search exceeded performance expectations  
* DDD bounded contexts made the complex domain manageable  
* Docker Compose provided consistent development environment  
* Agile with 2-week sprints enabled steady progress

**What was challenging:**

* OCR accuracy for poor-quality scanned CVs  
* LLM JSON parsing required multiple retry attempts  
* Distributed transactions required careful design  
* Frontend story estimation was consistently low

**What I would do differently:**

* Benchmark vector search performance earlier (not after integration)  
* Add health checks to all Docker services from Sprint 1  
* Document architectural decisions (ADRs) from the start  
* Allocate more time for documentation in each sprint

### **9.4.2 Personal Reflections**

**Blessing (Project Lead & AI/ML Engineer):**  
*"Leading this project taught me that AI is not just about models \- it's about understanding the domain deeply. The RAG pipeline worked because we understood how recruiters think, not because we had the fanciest model."*

**Gaudencio (Backend & Systems Architect):**  
*"Designing microservices with DDD was challenging but rewarding. The clear boundaries meant we could work in parallel without stepping on each other's toes. Event-driven architecture is powerful but requires discipline."*

**James (Frontend & UI/UX Designer):**  
*"Building interfaces for two different user types (candidates and recruiters) taught me the importance of role-based UX. The same component often needed different behaviour depending on who was using it."*

**Ozioma (Data Engineer & QA Lead):**  
*"The testing pyramid saved us. When we refactored the matching service, the unit tests caught breaking changes immediately. Without them, we would have introduced bugs that would have been hard to find."*

### **9.4.3 Team Reflection**

![][image30]

## **9.5 Final Conclusion**

This research set out to design, develop, and evaluate an AI-powered recruitment platform for Tumaini Consulting, a majority Black-owned recruitment agency in Cape Town, South Africa.

**The primary research question** asked how an AI-powered platform using RAG and vector databases could reduce manual CV screening time. The answer, demonstrated quantitatively, is a 90% reduction from 5-15 hours to 1.2 hours per role. This was achieved through automated CV parsing, semantic search, RAG-based matching, and automated shortlisting.

**The secondary research questions** were all addressed:

* The optimal DDD and microservices architecture comprises five bounded contexts  
* Semantic search achieves 89% recall vs 42% for keyword search  
* RAG provides explainable scores through natural-language rationales citing specific evidence  
* POPIA compliance is achievable using AWS af-south-1 and Llama 3 fallback  
* Agile Scrum with 2-week sprints delivered all 200 story points on schedule

**The contributions** are both academic and practical:

Academically, this research provides a documented case study of RAG for recruitment, DDD for the recruitment domain, South African NER enhancement, and POPIA-compliant AI architecture.

Practically, the deployed system is in use by Tumaini Consulting, processing thousands of CVs, reducing screening time by 90%, and achieving 96% adherence to the 3-day response standard.

**The name "Tumaini" means "Hope" in Swahili.** This project aimed to bring hope to:

* **Candidates:** Faster responses, transparent processes, fairer evaluation  
* **Recruiters:** Less fatigue, more time for meaningful human interaction  
* **Tumaini Consulting:** Scalable operations, enterprise-ready technology  
* **South African SMEs:** Open-source components, reference architecture

The evidence shows that hope is not just a word \- it is a measurable outcome. Through the application of Retrieval-Augmented Generation, vector databases, and thoughtful software architecture, this project transformed a manual, fatigue-driven operation into an intelligent, scalable talent acquisition engine.

*"Where there is hope, there is the potential for remarkable change and limitless possibilities."*
